touchcancel:JMtRjd;" jsshadow jsname="ipHvib" aria-label="Scroll down" aria-disabled="false" tabindex="0"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -12px"><svg class="XE8yyf" viewBox="0 0 24 24" focusable="false"><path d="M7.41 7.84L12 12.42l4.59-4.58L18 9.25l-6 6-6-6z"/><path d="M0-.75h24v24H0z" fill="none"/></svg></span></span></div></div></section><section id="h.140c560921aee500_92" class="yaqOZd" style=""><div class="IFuOkc"></div><div class="mYVXT"><div class="LS81yb VICjCf j5pSsc db35Fc" tabindex="-1"><div class="hJDwNd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd Ft7HRd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd purZT-AhqUyc-II5mzb ZcASvf-AhqUyc-II5mzb pSzOP-AhqUyc-qWD73c Ktthjf-AhqUyc-qWD73c JNdkSc SQVYQc"><div class="JNdkSc-SmKAyb LkDMRd"><div class="" jscontroller="sGwD4d" jsaction="zXBUYb:zTPCnb;zQF9Uc:Qxe3nd;" jsname="F57UId"><div class="oKdM2c ZZyype Kzv0Me"><div id="h.140c560921aee500_89" class="hJDwNd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd Ft7HRd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd jXK9ad D2fZ2 zu5uec OjCsFc dmUFtb wHaque g5GTcb JYTMs"><div class="jXK9ad-SmKAyb"><div class="tyJCtd mGzaTb Depvyb baZpAe"><p dir="ltr" class="CDt4Ke zfr3Q" style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 2.304; margin-bottom: 15pt; margin-top: 0; padding-bottom: 0; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0;"><span style="color: #0bd618; font-family: &#39;Comic Sans MS&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">ABOUT MY SHOWROOM</span><span style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Comic Sans MS&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-size: 14pt; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">:</span></p><p dir="ltr" class="CDt4Ke zfr3Q" style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 2.304; margin-bottom: 15pt; margin-top: 9pt; padding-bottom: 0; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0;"><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">Though laptops with displays that go beyond 1080p have only started popping up recently, they&#39;re already offered by a surprisingly wide selection of manufacturers. Most seem to settle on a resolution of 2560 by 1440 pixels (known as WQHD), while some manufacturers<a class="XqQF9c rXJpyf" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2013%2F12%2F13%2F5206170%2Fsamsung-ativ-book-9-plus-review&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw1fMVXSi0xrZ7eowKsKKgft" target="_blank"> </a></span><span class=" aw5Odc jgG6ef" style="font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"><a class="XqQF9c" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2013%2F12%2F13%2F5206170%2Fsamsung-ativ-book-9-plus-review&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw1fMVXSi0xrZ7eowKsKKgft" target="_blank">like Samsung</a></span><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"><a class="XqQF9c rXJpyf" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2014%2F2%2F5%2F5377754%2Flenovo-yoga-2-pro-review&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw3PuhXqvtTM12CtwJmxPp7v" target="_blank"> </a></span><span class=" jgG6ef aw5Odc" style="font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"><a class="XqQF9c" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2014%2F2%2F5%2F5377754%2Flenovo-yoga-2-pro-review&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw3PuhXqvtTM12CtwJmxPp7v" target="_blank">and Lenovo</a></span><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"> have opted to go even higher, jumping up to 3200 by 1800 pixels. That makes the effectively 4K resolution of 3840 by 2160 pixels on Toshiba&#39;s new Satellite P55t impressive, but not leaps and bounds ahead of the competition.</span></p><p dir="ltr" class="CDt4Ke zfr3Q" style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 2.304; margin-bottom: 15pt; margin-top: 0; padding-bottom: 0; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0;"><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">Its maximum specs do make it fairly compelling though: it has an i7 Haswell processor, includes a 1TB hard drive, and supports up to 16GB of RAM, a Blu-ray drive, and one of AMD&#39;s new Radeon R9 series laptop graphics units with 2GB of memory. Toshiba doesn&#39;t make it perfectly clear whether that specific GPU comes with the laptop at its base price â€” you can be sure a full 16GB of RAM doesn&#39;t â€” but whatever is powering the Satellite P55t&#39;s graphics may just make or break this laptop. It&#39;ll need something that&#39;s powerful enough to support those millions of pixels all without quickly wiping out its battery.</span></p><p dir="ltr" class="CDt4Ke zfr3Q" style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 2.304; margin-bottom: 15pt; margin-top: 0; padding-bottom: 0; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0;"><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">And with all those pixels, Toshiba is aiming the laptop toward photographers, even bundling in a copy of Lightroom 5 for photo editing. All said, it sounds compelling, though the laptop still has its shortcomings. For one, the Satellite P55t is no Ultrabook: if it has the same dimensions as Toshiba&#39;s seemingly identical P50t, which appears to be<a class="XqQF9c rXJpyf" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.toshiba.co.uk%2Fpress%2Freleases%2Fsatellite-p-series-2014%2F&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw1TxbLRHprXU9b125mh_1bA" target="_blank"> </a></span><span class=" jgG6ef aw5Odc" style="font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"><a class="XqQF9c" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.toshiba.co.uk%2Fpress%2Freleases%2Fsatellite-p-series-2014%2F&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw1TxbLRHprXU9b125mh_1bA" target="_blank">its previously announced UK counterpart</a></span><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">, the P55t will be about 1.1-inches thick and weigh a somewhat hefty 4.85 pounds.</span></p><p dir="ltr" class="CDt4Ke zfr3Q" style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 2.304; margin-bottom: 15pt; margin-top: 0; padding-bottom: 0; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0;"><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">Naturally, all of the high-res laptops right now seem to make some tradeoff between price, resolution, and size. We&#39;ve broken them down by resolution in the chart below, featuring models with WQHD resolution on the left and the higher 3200 by 1800 pixel resolution on the right. Even Toshiba itself offers one of the more compelling options competing for attention here,<a class="XqQF9c rXJpyf" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2014%2F1%2F6%2F5280034%2Ftoshiba-refreshes-its-kirabook-with-haswell-and-a-lower-1499-99-price&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw3_Eyp_FgOSTmkHUoVda_GU" target="_blank"> </a></span><span class=" jgG6ef aw5Odc" style="font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"><a class="XqQF9c" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2014%2F1%2F6%2F5280034%2Ftoshiba-refreshes-its-kirabook-with-haswell-and-a-lower-1499-99-price&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw3_Eyp_FgOSTmkHUoVda_GU" target="_blank">the Kirabook</a></span><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">. Because these are largely 13.3-inch laptops too, the higher-resolution options have nearly the same pixel density as the Satellite P55t anyway: them at 276 pixels per inch, and Toshiba at 282.</span></p><p dir="ltr" class="CDt4Ke zfr3Q" style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 30pt; margin-top: 30pt; padding-bottom: 0; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0;"><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Lobster&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">Gaming laptops upto 25% offer</span></p><p dir="ltr" class="CDt4Ke zfr3Q" style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 30pt; margin-top: 30pt; padding-bottom: 0; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0;"><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">That these laptops offer similarly high resolutions without the extra bulk is a huge plus, and will likely win the average buyer over. But there&#39;s a big catch on many of them when it comes to graphics, and that&#39;s where Toshiba&#39;s new Satellite could edge them out. When including the Radeon R9 series notebook GPU, the P55t should ber more than ready to take on the integrated HD Graphics and Iris graphics that come with the others. While Iris graphics have<a class="XqQF9c rXJpyf" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2013%2F5%2F1%2F4291820%2Fintels-new-iris-integrated-graphics-offer-double-or-triple-the&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw1ymeZ-6glRI_W8CUWJTqgq" target="_blank"> </a></span><span class=" jgG6ef aw5Odc" style="font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"><a class="XqQF9c" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2013%2F5%2F1%2F4291820%2Fintels-new-iris-integrated-graphics-offer-double-or-triple-the&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw1ymeZ-6glRI_W8CUWJTqgq" target="_blank">really stepped up performance</a></span><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">f beyond what most people have come to expect from an integrated GPU, discrete units still offer the opportunity for laptops to perform far better.</span></p><p dir="ltr" class="CDt4Ke zfr3Q" style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 2.304; margin-bottom: 15pt; margin-top: 0; padding-bottom: 0; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0;"><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">The Satellite&#39;s final high-res competition comes from Apple&#39;s MacBook Pros. As with smartphones, Apple actually has some of the less impressive pixel counts out there, really letting something like the Satellite stand out. What the MacBook Pros do have are<a class="XqQF9c rXJpyf" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2013%2F10%2F30%2F5044874%2F13-inch-macbook-pro-with-retina-display-review-2013&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw358ft12OvRRUJtDIdAVKQU" target="_blank"> </a></span><span class=" aw5Odc jgG6ef" style="font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"><a class="XqQF9c" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2013%2F10%2F30%2F5044874%2F13-inch-macbook-pro-with-retina-display-review-2013&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw358ft12OvRRUJtDIdAVKQU" target="_blank">nearly all-metal bodies and impressive build qualities</a></span><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"> that are hard to match. At the very high end,<a class="XqQF9c rXJpyf" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2013%2F10%2F24%2F5024346%2Fmacbook-pro-with-retina-display-review-15-inch-2013&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw3xYQxro8pDVx_iJFC-wqYM" target="_blank"> </a></span><span class=" jgG6ef aw5Odc" style="font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"><a class="XqQF9c" href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2F2013%2F10%2F24%2F5024346%2Fmacbook-pro-with-retina-display-review-15-inch-2013&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AOvVaw3xYQxro8pDVx_iJFC-wqYM" target="_blank">the 15-inch model</a></span><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"> includes an option for discrete graphics with 2GB of memory too â€” it&#39;s a pricier option, but a compelling one if you&#39;re not sold on the difference in resolution once pixel density is that high.</span></p><p dir="ltr" class="CDt4Ke zfr3Q" style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 2.304; margin-bottom: 15pt; margin-top: 0; padding-bottom: 0; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0;"><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Georgia&#39;, &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">Now that it&#39;s here, it&#39;s hard to imagine that we won&#39;t soon start seeing more and more 4K displays built inside of laptops. It may be a little while before they come down to thinner ones such as Apple&#39;s MacBook Pros, but manufacturers like Toshiba and Razer show that plenty is possible, even in a small body.</span></p><p dir="ltr" class="CDt4Ke zfr3Q" style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 30pt; margin-top: 30pt; padding-bottom: 0; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0;"><span class=" jgG6ef" style="color: #ffffff; font-family: &#39;Arial&#39;; font-weight: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">FEATURED</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></section></div><div class="Xpil1b xgQ6eb"></div><footer jsname="yePe5c" class="yxgWrb "><section id="h.23c89aac75c39ea_6" class="yaqOZd" style=""><div class="IFuOkc"></div><div class="mYVXT"><div class="LS81yb VICjCf j5pSsc db35Fc" tabindex="-1"><div class="hJDwNd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd Ft7HRd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd purZT-AhqUyc-II5mzb ZcASvf-AhqUyc-II5mzb pSzOP-AhqUyc-qWD73c Ktthjf-AhqUyc-qWD73c JNdkSc SQVYQc"><div class="JNdkSc-SmKAyb LkDMRd"><div class="" jscontroller="sGwD4d" jsaction="zXBUYb:zTPCnb;zQF9Uc:Qxe3nd;" jsname="F57UId"><div class="oKdM2c ZZyype Kzv0Me"><div id="h.23c89aac75c39ea_3" class="hJDwNd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd Ft7HRd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd jXK9ad D2fZ2 zu5uec OjCsFc dmUFtb wHaque g5GTcb JYTMs"><div class="jXK9ad-SmKAyb"><div class="tyJCtd mGzaTb Depvyb baZpAe"><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR" style="list-style-type: square;
